									<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>Sarkari Naukri,</strong></span> or <span style="color: #800080;"><strong>government jobs, </strong></span>recruitment processes may be different for each and every post in India. Some exams are one-day exams; some exams for Sarkari Naukri are conducted in three stages: <strong><span style="color: #008000;">Prelims, Mains and Interview</span>. </strong>The general process of recruitment is this: </p><ul><li>Release of Recruitment Notification.</li><li>Filling Out the Application Form.</li><li>Issuing Admit Card Or Hall Ticket </li><li>Conducting Exam ( Prelims, Mains Or Maybe One Day Exam ) </li><li>Releasing Written Result </li><li>Shortlisting Candidates For Interview </li><li>Releasing Final Merit List </li></ul>								</div>
